$(function() {
var searchHeader = $('#header_search_form');
var searchInput = searchHeader.find('input[name="q"]');
var searchSuggestField = searchHeader.find('.suggest__field');
if (!searchHeader.length) {
return;
}
searchInput.on('focus', function() {
searchSuggestField.addClass('focus');
}).on('blur', function() {
searchSuggestField.removeClass('focus');
});
var autocompleteNameSpace = 'ui-autocomplete';
var autocompleteRequest = '/search/suggest';
function getSearchItems(requestTerm, callback) {
if (!requestTerm.length) {
searchInput.autocomplete('close');
return;
}
$.ajax({
type: 'get',
url: autocompleteRequest,
data: {
term: requestTerm
},
success: callback
});
}
function setWidthSearchItems() {
var widthWindow = $(window).width();
var widthTable = 768;
var widthForInput = searchSuggestField.outerWidth();
if (widthWindow >= widthTable) {
$('.' + autocompleteNameSpace + ':visible').css('width', widthForInput);
}
}
function chooseItemWithEnter(e, ui) {
var event = e.originalEvent;
var url = ui.item.url;
var enter = 13;
if (event.keyCode === enter)
window.location.href = url;
return false;
}
var autocompleteCreate = searchInput.autocomplete({
minLength: 0,
position: {
my: 'left top+5',
at: 'left bottom'
},
source: function(request, response) {
getSearchItems(request.term, response);
},
open: setWidthSearchItems,
select: chooseItemWithEnter,
focus: function(event, ui) {
return false;
}
});
autocompleteCreate.data(autocompleteNameSpace)._renderItem = function(ul, item) {
var autocompleteMainClass = 'autocomplete_main';
var bu = $('meta[name="sbu"]', document.head).attr('content');
var imageTemplates = {
imageUserBase: '<svg class="icon_suggest icon_userpic" viewBox="0 0 32 32"><use href="' + bu + 'images/sprite.svg#icon_userpic"></use></svg>',
imageUserFixed: '<img class="icon_suggest icon_avatar-img" src="' + item.avatar + '" />',
imageTagBase: '<svg class="icon_suggest icon_tag_small" viewBox="0 0 32 32"><use href="' + bu + 'images/sprite.svg#icon_tag"></use></svg>',
imageTagFxed: '<img class="icon_suggest icon_tag-img" src="' + item.image_url + '" />'
};
ul.addClass(autocompleteMainClass);
userImage = item.avatar ? imageTemplates.imageUserFixed : imageTemplates.imageUserBase;
tagImage = item.image_url ? imageTemplates.imageTagFxed : imageTemplates.imageTagBase;
function createNodeElement(image, tag, content) {
return image + '<' + tag + '>' + content + '</' + tag + '>';
}
var searchString = '';
if (item.type === 'user') {
searchString = createNodeElement(userImage, 'span', item.label);
} else if (item.type === 'tag') {
searchString = createNodeElement(tagImage, 'span', item.label);
} else if (item.type === 'search') {
var content = 'Ð’ÑÐµ Ñ€ÐµÐ·ÑƒÐ»ÑŒÑ‚Ð°Ñ‚Ñ‹ Ð¿Ð¾ Ð·Ð°Ð¿Ñ€Ð¾ÑÑƒ ' + 'Â«' + item.label + 'Â»';
searchString = createNodeElement('', 'strong', content);
} else {
searchString = item.label;
}
var forAppendItem = '<li class="ui-search-type-' + item.type + '">';
var forAppendLink = '<a href="' + item.url + '">' + searchString + '</a>';
var renderedList = $(forAppendItem).append(forAppendLink).appendTo(ul);
return renderedList;
}
;
});
window.add_event_to_analytics = function() {
var analyticsEvents = {
questions_similar: {
action: 'question_similar_click',
category: 'context_block',
},
questions_most: {
action: 'interesting_question_click',
category: 'context_block',
},
tags_similar: {
action: 'tags_similar_click',
category: 'context_block',
},
tags_popular: {
action: 'tags_popular_click',
category: 'context_block',
},
user_popular: {
action: 'users_active_click',
category: 'context_block',
}
};
var queryObject = window.create_query_string_parts(location.search);
if (!queryObject.from) {
return;
}
function removeQueryStringFromLocation() {
window.history.replaceState('', '', location.pathname);
}
function getdataAnalytics(data) {
return {
category: data.category,
action: data.action,
label: document.referrer
}
}
var currentObjcet = analyticsEvents[queryObject.from];
function sendDataAnalytics(data) {
safe_ga_event(data.category, data.action, data.label);
}
var dataAnalytics = getdataAnalytics(currentObjcet);
sendDataAnalytics(dataAnalytics);
if (window.history) {
removeQueryStringFromLocation();
}
}
;
window.add_event_to_analytics();
$(function() {
$(document).on('click', '[data-watch-tag]', function() {
var btn = $(this);
var act = btn.data('watch-tag');
var url = '/my/wtag_' + (act == 'u' ? 'unsub' : 'sub');
var data = {
tag_id: btn.data('tid')
};
$.post({
url: url,
data: data,
dataType: 'json',
headers: {
'x-form-token': $(this).data('token-' + act)
},
success: function(resp) {
btn.toggleClass('btn_active', act == 's');
btn.data('watch-tag', act == 's' ? 'u' : 's');
btn.find('span:eq(0)').html(resp.hl_msg.lbl).attr('title', resp.hl_msg.title);
btn.find('.btn__counter').html(resp.hl_msg.cnt);
if (act == 's') {
safe_ga_event('subscription', 'tag_subscription', resp.tname);
}
;
}
}).fail(function(xhr) {
showFlashMessage(xhr.responseJSON.error.msg, 'warning');
});
});

btn.nextAll('.dropdown__menu').find('input[data-force-watch-tag]').prop('checked', false);
if (act == 's') {
safe_ga_event('subscription', 'tag_subscription', resp.tname);
}
;var cntr = $('@subscribers_counter');
cntr.html(parseInt(cntr.text()) + (act == 's' ? 1 : -1));

tag_template.find('.card__head-image_tag img').replaceWith(svg_icon);
}
;var render_tag = function(tag, container) {
var new_tag = tag_template.clone();
new_tag.find('.card__head-title > a').attr('href', tag.url).attr('title', tag.name).html(tag.display_name);
new_tag.find('.card__stats-counter').attr('href', tag.url + '/questions').html(tag.questions_count_text);

}
;container.after(new_tag);
};
var render_tags = function(tags, container) {
var i = tags.length;
do {
var tag = tags[--i];
if ($('#subscribe_link_' + tag.id).length) {
continue;
}
;render_tag(tag, container);
} while (i);
};
var always_on_resp = function(resp) {
if (resp.now_watching >= resp.need_watch) {
$('@progree_complete').removeClass('hidden');
$('@progree_non_complete').addClass('hidden');
} else if (resp.now_watching < resp.need_watch) {
$('@progree_complete').addClass('hidden');
$('@progree_non_complete').removeClass('hidden');
$('.progress__counter').html(resp.now_watching + '/' + resp.need_watch);
$('.progress').data('progress', Math.round(resp.now_watching / resp.need_watch * 100));
moveProgressBar();
}
;
};
$(document).on('click', '[data-ftw-tag]', function() {
var tag_id = $(this).data('ftw-tag');
var container = $(this).closest('.content-list__item');
var tag_name = container.find('.card__head-title > a').attr('title');
$.post({
url: 'tags/ft_watch',
data: {
tag_id: tag_id
},
dataType: 'json',
headers: {
'x-form-token': $(this).data('token-w')
},
success: function(resp) {
always_on_resp(resp);
$('#subscribe_link_' + tag_id).addClass('btn_active').removeAttr('data-ftw-tag').attr('data-ftu-tag', tag_id).find('span:first').html('Ð’Ñ‹ Ð¿Ð¾Ð´Ð¿Ð¸ÑÐ°Ð½Ñ‹');
$('#subscribe_link_' + tag_id + ' .btn__counter').html(resp.tag_watchers_count_text);
render_tags(resp.tags, container);
safe_ga_event('subscription', 'tag_subscription', tag_name);
}
}).fail(function(xhr) {
showFlashMessage(xhr.responseJSON.error.msg, 'warning');
});
});

url: '/answer/' + act,
data: {
answer_id: aid
},
dataType: 'json',
headers: {
'x-form-token': btn.data('token-' + act[0])
},
success: function(resp) {
btn.data('approve-answer', act == 'approve' ? 'u' : 'a');
btn.toggleClass('btn_active', act == 'approve');
btn.html(resp.hl_msg.lbl);
if (!resp.is_vs && resp.success) {
var tlist = act == 'approve' ? '#solutions_list' : '#answers_list';
$('#answer_item_' + aid).appendTo(tlist);
answersCount();
$('@solutions_section').toggleClass('hidden', $('#solutions_list @answer_item').length == 0);
$('@answers_section').toggleClass('hidden', $('#answers_list @answer_item').length == 0);
$('#answer_' + aid + ' .answer').toggleClass('answer_solution', act == 'approve');
}
;if (act == 'approve' && resp.success) {
safe_ga_event('question', 'solution_created', resp.author_username);
}
;
}
}).fail(function(xhr) {
alert('fail :(');
});
});
});

;

;function display_yandex_rtb(yandexId, divId) {
$('#' + divId).show();
(function(w, d, n, s, t) {
w[n] = w[n] || [];
w[n].push(function() {
Ya.Context.AdvManager.render({
blockId: yandexId,
renderTo: divId,
async: true
});
});
t = d.getElementsByTagName('script')[0];
s = d.createElement('script');
s.type = 'text/javascript';
s.src = '//an.yandex.ru/system/context.js';
s.async = true;
t.parentNode.insertBefore(s, t);
}
)(this, this.document, 'yandexContextAsyncCallbacks');
}
;function listen_googletag_and_render_yandex(yandexId, targetDivId) {
if (!window.googletag || !window.googletag.cmd) {
return;
}
;window.googletag.cmd.push(function() {
if (!window.googletag.pubads) {
return;
}
;window.googletag.pubads().addEventListener('slotRenderEnded', function(event) {
var divId = event.slot.getSlotElementId();
if (divId === targetDivId && event.isEmpty) {
display_yandex_rtb(yandexId, divId);
}
;
});
});
}
;var roxot = function() {
var pmap = {
'gid': 10000,
'sid': 100,
'deep': 100
};
var get = function(p) {
try {
var key = 'roxot-' + p;
var val = window.localStorage.getItem(key);
if (val === null) {
val = 1 + Math.floor(Math.random() * pmap[p]);
window.localStorage.setItem(key, val);
}
;return val;
} catch (e) {
return pmap[p] + 1;
}
;
};
this.group = function() {
return get('gid');
}
;
this.sector = function() {
return get('sid');
}
;
this.deep = function() {
return get('deep');
}
;
};
var urls = {
google: 'https://www.googletagservices.com/tag/js/gpt.js',
criteo: 'https://static.criteo.net/js/ld/publishertag.js'
};
var load_js = function(url) {
var dfd = $.Deferred();
var s = document.createElement('script');
s.async = true;
s.src = url;
s.onload = function() {
dfd.resolve();
}
;
document.head.appendChild(s);
return dfd.promise();
};
var def_map = function(gtag) {
var m = [];
m['TS01_ATF'] = gtag.sizeMapping().addSize([1024, 600], [[300, 600], [300, 500], [300, 300], [300, 250]]).addSize([0, 0], []).build();
m['TS02_horizonal'] = gtag.sizeMapping().addSize([1440, 800], [[830, 240], [830, 166]]).addSize([1360, 768], [[750, 240], [750, 192], [750, 150]]).addSize([1280, 700], [[670, 240], [670, 150]]).addSize([1200, 640], [590, 200]).addSize([1024, 600], [664, 166]).addSize([0, 0], []).build();

var def_slot = function(id, gtag, map) {

};
var set_target = function(gtag) {
$('#dfp_target > var').each(function(idx, item) {
var name = $(item).data('name');
var values = $(item).data('values').toString().split(',');
gtag.pubads().setTargeting(name, values);
});
var rx = new roxot();
var dt = new Date();
var chr = dt.getHours();
var cwd = ['su', 'mo', 'tu', 'we', 'th', 'fr', 'sa'][dt.getDay()];
gtag.pubads().setTargeting('roxot-group-id', rx.group()).setTargeting('roxot-sector-id', rx.sector()).setTargeting('roxot-deep', rx.deep()).setTargeting('chr', (chr > 9 ? '' : '0') + chr).setTargeting('cwd', cwd);
};
var show_banners = function(banner_funcs) {

});

def_slot(item.id, gtag, map);
});

gtag.pubads().collapseEmptyDivs();
banner_funcs.targeting(gtag);
gtag.enableServices();
});
ymap = banner_funcs.ynd_map();
dfp_banners.each(function(idx, item) {

;gtag.cmd.push(function() {
gtag.display(item.id);
});
});
gtag.cmd.push(function() {
banner_funcs.after(gtag);
});
};
var aa_detect = function() {
var check_image = function(num) {
var dfd = $.Deferred();
var img = new Image();
img.onload = function() {
dfd.resolve(true);
}
;
img.onerror = function() {
dfd.resolve(false);
}
;
img.src = '/images/px.gif?ch=' + num + '&rn=' + (Math.random() * 11);
return dfd.promise();
};
return $.when(check_image(1), check_image(2)).then(function(r1, r2) {
return r1 && !r2;
});
};

};

};
};

var crt_banner_funcs = function(dflt_funcs, ad_units) {

},

crt.SetDFPKeyValueTargeting();
gtag.pubads().refresh();
};
crt.events.push(function() {
crt.SetLineItemRanges("0..599:1;600..1398:2;1400..3000:5");
crt.RequestBids(ad_units, launch, 500);
});
}
};
};

var DOCUMENT = $(document);
function initViewer(element) {
var config = {
inline: false,
navbar: false,
title: true,
toolbar: false,
};
return new Viewer(element,config);
}
function containImage(selector) {
return $(selector).filter(function(key, element) {
return $(element).has('img').length;
});
}
function toFilter(selectors) {
return selectors.map(function(value) {
return containImage(value).toArray();
});
}
function toFlat(selectors) {
return selectors.reduce(function(accum, element) {
return accum.concat(element);
}, []);
}
function initImages() {
var selectors = ['.js-answer-text, .js-comment-text, .js-question-text'];
var selectorsFiltered = toFilter(selectors);
var selectorsFlat = toFlat(selectorsFiltered);
selectorsFlat.forEach(function(element) {
initViewer(element);
});
}
DOCUMENT.ready(initImages);

}).then(resp=>resp.json()).then(resp=>{
for (t in resp.results) {

if (r.hasOwnProperty('adverts') && r.adverts.length) {
show[t](r.adverts);
}
;
}
;registerEvents();
}
);
function makeQueries() {

queries.ft = {
type: 'featurer',
count: 1,
view: {
lang: 'ru'
}
};
}
;if ($('#habr_effect_megapost').length) {
queries.mp = {
type: 'megapost',
count: 1,
filter: {
langs: ['ru']
}
};
}
;if ($('#habr_effect_promo').length) {
queries.pp = {
type: 'promopost',
count: 3,
filter: {
langs: ['ru']
},
view: {
lang: 'ru'
}
};
}
;return queries;
}
;var show = {
ft: (adverts)=>{
var tpl = $('#habr_effect_featurer');
var el = $(tpl.html());
var adv = adverts[0];
el.find('a').attr('href', adv.link.url).attr('data-featurer-ga', adv.gal);
el.find('img').attr('src', adv.image.url).attr('alt', adv.title).after(adv.title);
tpl.replaceWith(el);
}
,
mp: (adverts)=>{

tpl.replaceWith(el);
events.push(adv.events.view);
}
,
pp: (adverts)=>{
function makeItem(itpl, data) {
var item = $(itpl);
item.find('a').attr('href', data.link.url);
item.find('.habr-block-megaposts__image').css('background-image', 'url(' + data.image.url + ')');
item.find('.habr-block-megaposts__text').html(data.title);
item.find('.habr-block-megaposts__label').prepend(data.label);
if (data.external) {
item.find('a').attr('rel', 'nofollow sponsored');
} else {
item.find('.external_link').remove();
}
;return item;
}
;var tpl = $('#habr_effect_promo');
var el = $(tpl.html());

});

}
};

}
;
}
)(document, window, "yandex_metrika_callbacks");
}
